Jamison Brereton

65 (891)
All Gods
Vasukarс╣Зa V─Бsukra
15 verses: jagat─л, except triс╣гс╣нubh 15
The poetic pedigree sketched above gives us high expectations for the hymn, which, however, begins unpromisingly with a simple enumeration of gods. Nonetheless, although the style never achieves the same distinction as that of the poetтАЩs putative relatives, there are many nice touches and twists and turns of syntax, particularly in verses 2тАУ8, treating the cosmogonic deeds of the gods and the praise and sacrifice offered to them by mortals.
The hymn seems to begin anew with verse 9, which contains another straightfor ward listing of gods, continued in verse 10. A brief account of cosmogony (vs. 11) is followed by a sketch of the A┼ЫvinsтАЩ deeds (vs. 12). Minor gods join the undifferentiated mass of All Gods in verses 13тАУ14, and the hymn ends with Vasiс╣гс╣нhaтАЩs summary verse.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬIndra, and Agni, the lords of the virtuous, standing in the same plural ce, mutually invigorating each otherwith might in the Vс╣Ыtra-slaying battles, and the gh─л-glorified Soma putting forth his greatness have filled the vastfirmament with their strength.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Gh─л-glorified: ghс╣Ыta┼Ыr─л = having recourse to the Vasat─лvari water

Jamison Brereton

Indra and Agni, the two lords of the settlement, spurring each other on mutually in the smashing of obstacles, sharing the same homeтАФ
they (all) filled the great midspace with their might, as did Soma,
glorious with ghee, rousing their greatness.

Griffith

Indra and Agni, Hero-lords when Vrtra fell, dwelling together, speeding emulously on,
And Soma blent with oil, putting his greatness forth, have with their power filled full the mighty firmament.

Geldner

Indra und Agni, die rechten Herren, die in den Vritrak├дmpfen sich gegenseitig selbst anspornen, die Hausgenossen, sie alle haben mit ihrer Kraft den gro├Яen Luftraum erf├╝llt, und Soma, der Schmalzgemischte, der ihre Macht hervorbringt.

Grassmann

Die Helden Indra, Agni in der Vritraschlacht, einander f├╢rdernd, miteinander engvereint, Durchdrangen ganz die weite Luft mit ihrer Kraft; der fettgemischte Soma steigert ihre Macht.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬSkilled in pious rites, I recite the praises of these (deities), mighty through (their own) might,unassailable, exalted by sacrifice; may those (gods) who possessed of various wealth, (rain down) the beautifulwater-cloud, acting in friendly wise, grant us (wealth) for our honour (among men).тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

For by the greatness of these, the great and unassailable, I, recognizing the truth, rouse my praises for those who grow strong through truth.
Let those who are bringing brilliant bounties (across) the watery flood grant them to us. I magnify the (heavenly clans) well allied (to us).

Griffith

Skilled in the Law I lift the hymn of praise to these, Law-strengtheners, unassailed, and great in majesty.
These in their wondrous bounty send the watery sea: may they as kindly Friends send gifts to make us great.

Geldner

Denn auf diese an Gr├╢├Яe Gro├Яen und Unerreichten lasse ich die Loblieder aufsteigen, ich der Wahrheitskenner auf die Wahrheitsmehrer, die wunderbare Gaben haben, die die Wasserflut spenden, die sollen uns schenken, um unseren Mut zu erh├╢hen, gute Freundschaft haltend.

Grassmann

Denn ich erweck’ mit Macht ihr Lob, der M├дchtigen, rechtskundig der erhabnen, die des Rechts sich freun, Die vielfach spendend wasserreiche Flut verleihn, die m├╢gen freundlich uns zum Gl├╝ck beh├╝lflich sein.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬThey have sustained by their strength the leader of all (the sun), the luminaries of the firmament,heaven and earth, the outstretched (firmament), honouring (their worshippers) like those who give food (to thepoor), the genitive rous gods bestowing wealth on man are glorified (at this sacrifice).тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Those who give food to thepoor: bringing riches into contact with the poor; derived from pс╣Ыc, to touch

Jamison Brereton

They propped up (the region) of solar glory, the midspaces, the realms of light, Heaven and Earth, the Broad One, with their might.
Magnifying (them), bringing lovely gifts like strengthening
nourishments, the gods are praised as patrons to the race of Manu.

Griffith

They with their might have stayed Heaven, Earth, and Prthivi, the Lord of Light, the firmament, -the lustrous spheres.
Even as fleet-foot steeds who make their masters glad, the princely Gods are praised, most bountiful to man.

Geldner

Svarnara, die Luftr├дume, die Lichtr├дume, Himmel und Erde, das Land haben sie mit Kraft gest├╝tzt. Die freigebig wie die lebenskr├дftigen Angiras den Mut erh├╢hen, die G├╢tter werden als G├╢nner f├╝r den Menschen gepriesen.

Grassmann

Den Glanzesherrn, die L├╝fte und des Lichtes Raum, den Himmel und die Erde st├╝tzten sie mit Macht; Es preist der Mensch die G├╢tter, sie die leuchtenden, wie Rosse, die mit Schatz beladen hoch erfreun.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬWorship the liberal Mitra and Varuс╣Зa, the two royal deities who are never negligent in their thoughts,whose vast body is resplendent through their functions, upon whom the two solicitous worlds (heaven and earth)remain (dependent).тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Their functions: of illuminating the world; two solicitous worlds: n─Бdhasi = solicitous; or,abounding in gods and men

Jamison Brereton

Try your utmost for Mitra and for Varuс╣Зa who does ritual service, the two sovereign kings who do not stay distant in their thought,
whose lofty domain shines by reason of their ordinance, for whom the two world-halves are two opposing troops in need of help.

Griffith

Bring gifts to Mitra and to Varuna who, Lords of all, in spirit never fail the worshipper,
Whose statute shines on high through everlasting Law, whose places of sure refuge are the heavens and earth.

Geldner

Mache es Mitra und Varuna recht, den beiden Allk├╢nigen, die gegen den Spender im Geiste nie gleichg├╝ltig werden, deren hohe Sch├╢pfung nach ihrer Bestimmung strahlt, denen die beiden Welten Schutztruppe und Gefolge sind.

Grassmann

Dem Mitra spende und dem treuen Varuna, den Herrschern, die mit ihrem Geist nicht ferne sind, Sie, deren St├дtte durch Gerechtigkeit ergl├дnzt, und denen Erd’ und Himmel H├╝lfe flehend nahn.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay that cow, the leader of the rite, which yielding her milk proceeds uncalled to the consecratedplace (of sacrifice), may she, propitiated by me, yield her milk to (me), the offerer of oblations to liberal Varuс╣Зaand the (other) gods.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Milk: of strength, gauс╕е = thunder, m─Бdhyamik─Б v─Бk; cf. RV 8.100.11; offer of oblations:vivasvati = madhyam dev─Бn paricarate;

D─Б┼Ыuс╣гe = an epithet of Varuс╣Зa

Jamison Brereton

The cow [=offering ladle?] that goes around the (ritual) track to the appointed place, giving her milk, leading at the commandment (of
Varuс╣Зa), not by choice,
she, being announced, will do ritual service to Varuс╣Зa who (also) serves, to the gods, and to Vivasvant with the oblation.

Griffith

The cow who yielding milk goes her appointed way hither to us as leader of holy rites,
Speaking aloud to Varuna and the worshipper, shall with oblation serve Vivasvan and the Gods.

Geldner

Die Kuh, die die Bahn umwandelt zu dem Treffort, ihre Milch spendend, die Vorschrift ausf├╝hrend, ohne sich etwas auszubitten, sie, die das Opfer anmeldet, ist gegen Varuna, den Spender, gegen die G├╢tter und Vivasvat mit Opfer freigebig.

Grassmann

Die Kuh, durchwandernd den ihr angewiesnen Pfad, das Werk vollbringend, Milch ergiessend zu uns her; Sich selbst verk├╝ndend ihm, dem treuen Varuna, so dien’ mit Trank den G├╢ttern, dem Vivasvat sie.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬPervading heaven (with their radiance), having Agni as their tongue, the augmenters of sacrifice,(these deities) sit contemplating the plural ce of sacrifice; sustaining heaven they have produced the waters by theirpower; having genitive rated sacrifice, they have decorated their person ns (with it).тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

I.e., they partake of the oblation

Jamison Brereton

Those ruling over heaven, with Agni as their tongue, growing strong through truth, sit stroking the womb of truth.
Having propped up heaven, they brought the waters here by their might. Having given birth to the sacrifice, they clasped it to themselves.

Griffith

The Gods whose tongue is Agni dwell in heaven, and sit, aiders of Law, reflecting, in the seat of Law.
They propped up heaven and then brought waters with their might, got sacrifice and in a body made it fair.

Geldner

Die Himmelsbewohner, deren Zunge Agni ist, die Wahrheitsmehrer, sitzen da, den Scho├Я der Wahrheit bef├╝hlend, ├╝berdenkend. Den Himmel haben sie gest├╝tzt und mit Kraft die Wasser hergebracht. Sie haben das Opfer erschaffen und haben es sich selbst zugeeignet.

Grassmann

Mit Agni’s Zunge trinkend, himmlisch, reingesinnt, des Heiligthumes Schooss ber├╝hrend, sitzen sie; Den Himmel st├╝tzten kr├дftig sie, ergossen Flut, erzeugten Opfer, f├╝hrten dann es in den Leib.

English translation:

тАЬThe encompassing parents (heaven and earth), born of old, having a common dwelling, sit down uponthe plural ce of sacrifice; engaged in a common observance they sprinkle upon the adorable Varuс╣Зa water mixedwith butter.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

The two parents born of old, encircling, sharing the same home, rule in the womb of truth:
Heaven and Earth, who obey the same commandment to Varuс╣Зa, swell the ghee-filled milk for Varuс╣Зa, the buffalo.

Griffith

Born in the oldest time, the Parents dwelling round are sharers of one mansion in the home of Law.
Bound by their common vow Dyaus, Prthivi stream forth the moisture rich in oil to Varuna the Steer.

Geldner

Die ringsum wohnenden, erstgeborenen Eltern, die Hausgenossen herrschen im Scho├Яe der Wahrheit, Himmel und Erde, die dem Varuna in gleicher Weise botm├д├Яig sind, quellen f├╝r den B├╝ffel die schmalzige Milch.

Grassmann

Das Aelternpaar, das urgeboren ringsum wohnt, es sitzt vereinigt hier im Schooss des Heiligthums, In gleichem Dienst ergiessen Erd’ und Himmel Trank, den nahrungsreichen f├╝r den Varuna, den Stier.

Griffith

Parjanya, Vata, mighty, senders of the rain, Indra and Vayu, Varuna, Mitra, Aryaman:
We call on Aditi, Adityas, and the Gods, those who are on the earth, in waters, and in heaven.

Geldner

Parjanya und Vata, die wasserquellenden Bullen, Indra und Vayu, Varuna, Mitra, Aryaman. - Die G├╢tter Aditya┬┤s, Aditi rufen wir, die irdischen G├╢tter, die himmlischen und die im Wasser sind.

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬgenitive rating food, cows, horses, plural nts, trees, the earth, mountains and waters, elevating the sun inheaven, munificent, promoting sacred observances upon the earth, (they abide everywhere).тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

Genitive rating food:brahman = vс╣Ыdh to sustain, foster

Jamison Brereton

Those of good gifts, begetting the sacred formulation, the cow, the horse, the plants, the trees, the earth, the mountains, the waters,
causing the sun to mount in heaven, loosing the ─АryasтАЩ commandments upon the earth.

Griffith

They generated prayer, the cow, the horse, the plants, the forest trees, the earth, the waters, and the hills.
These very bounteous Gods made the Sun mount to heaven, and spread the righteous laws of Aryas o’er the land.

English translation:

тАЬYou, A┼Ыvins, extricated Bhujyu from calamity, you gave to Vadhrimat─л her son ┼Ъy─Бva; you gaveKamadyu (as a wife) to Vimada; you restored (the lost) Viс╣гс╣З─Бpu to Vi┼Ыvaka.тАЭ

Commentary by S─Бyaс╣Зa: с╣Ъgveda-bh─Бс╣гya

From calamity: from the sea, cf.RV 1.118.6;

Vidhrimat─л: son is called hiraс╣Зyahasta; cf. RV 1.117.24;

Kamadhyu = light of love, k─Бmasya d─лpti;

Viс╣гс╣З─Бpu: cf. RV 1.116.23; viс╣гс╣Зv─Бpya?

Jamison Brereton

You rescue Bhujyu from difficult straits, o A┼Ыvins. You gave life to ┼Ъy─Бva, the son of Vadhrimat─л.
You carried Kamady┼л to Vimada. You let loose Viс╣гс╣З─Бp┼л for Vi┼Ыvaka.

Griffith

O Asvins, ye delivered Bhujyu from distress, ye animated Syava, Vadhrmati’s son.
To Vimada ye brought his consort Kamadyu, and gave his lost Visnapu back to Visvaka.

Ihr Asvin helfet dem Bhujyu aus Not. Den Syava, der Vadhrimati Sohn, belebtet ihr. Dem Vimada f├╝hrtet ihr die Kamadyu zu; ihr gebet dem Visvaka den Visnapu frei.

рдкрд╛рд╡реАрд░рд╡реА рдЖрдпреБрдзрд╡рддреА рддрдиреНрдпрддреБрдГ рд╕реНрддрдирдпрд┐рддреНрд░реА рд╡рд╛рдЧреНрдорд╛рдзреНрдпрдорд┐рдХрд╛ рддрдерд╛ рджрд┐рд╡рдГ рджреНрдпреБрд▓реЛрдХрд╕реНрдп рдзрд░реНрддрд╛ рдзрд╛рд░рдпрд┐рддрд╛ рдЕрдЬрдГ рдПрдХрдкрд╛рддреН рдПрдХ рдПрд╡ рдкрджреНрдпрддреЗ рдЧрдЪреНрдЫрддреАрддрд┐ рди рдЬрд╛рдпрдд рдЗрддреНрдпреЗрддрддреНрд╕рдВрдЬреНрдЮрдХреЛ рджреЗрд╡рдГ рд╕рд┐рдиреНрдзреБрдГ рдЪ рд╕рдореБрджреНрд░рд┐рдпрдГ ред рд╕рдореБрджреНрд░рдордиреНрддрд░рд┐рдХреНрд╖рдореН ред рддрддреНрд░ рднрд╡рд╛рдГ рдЖрдкрдГ рдЪ ред тАШ рд╕рдореБрджреНрд░рд╛рднреНрд░рд╛рджреНрдзрдГ’ рдЗрддрд┐ рднрд╡рд╛рд░реНрдереЗ рдШрдкреНрд░рддреНрдпрдпрдГ ред рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡реЗ рджреЗрд╡рд╛рд╢реНрдЪ рдзреАрднрд┐рдГ рдХрд░реНрдорднрд┐рд░реНрдпреБрдХреНрддрд╛рдГ рдкреБрд░рдВрдзреНрдпрд╛ рдмрд╣реБрд╡рд┐рдзрдпрд╛ рдкреНрд░рдЬреНрдЮрдпрд╛ рд╕рд╣рд┐рддрд╛ рд╕рд░рд╕реНрд╡рддреА рдЪ рдореЗ рдорджреАрдпрд╛рдирд┐ рд╡рдЪрд╛рдВрд╕рд┐ рд╡рдХреНрддрд╡реНрдпрд╛рдирд┐ рд╕реНрддреЛрддреНрд░рд╛рдгрд┐ рд╢реГрдгрд╡рдиреН рд╢реГрдгреНрд╡рдиреНрддреБ ред тАШ рдкрд╡рд┐рдГ рд╢рд▓реНрдпреЛ рднрд╡рддрд┐ рдпрджреНрд╡рд┐рдкреБрдирд╛рддрд┐ рдХрд╛рдпрдореН ред ( рдирд┐рд░реБ. резреи.рейреж ) рдЗрддреНрдпрд╛рджрд┐ рдирд┐рд░реБрдХреНрддрдордиреБрд╕рдВрдзреЗрдпрдореН рее

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay the armed and thundering (voice of mid-heaven), the upholder of heaven, Aja Ekap─Бd, theocean, the waters of the firmament, the universal gods and Sarasvat─л, accompanied by sacred rites, andabundant wisdom, hear my words.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

The daughter of Pav─лru, Thunder, and Aja Ekapad, the supporter of heaven, the river, and the waters of the seaтАФ
all the gods will hear my words: (they and also) Sarasvat─л, along with insights [/Dh─л] and with plenty [/Puraс╣Гdh─л].

Griffith

Thunder, the lightning’s daughter, Aja-Ekapad, heaven’s bearer, Sindhu, and the waters of the sea:
Hear all the Gods my words, Sarasvati give ear together with Purandhi and with Holy Thoughts.

Geldner

Des Paviru Tochter, der Donner, der ungeborene Einfu├Я, der Tr├дger des Himmels, Sindhu, die Meeresgew├дsser, alle G├╢tter m├╢gen meine Worte erh├╢ren, Sarasvati nebst den frommen Gedanken und der Purandhi.

Grassmann

Der blitzversehne Donner und der Kreiselwind, des Himmels Tr├дger, Strom und Flut im Meer der Luft, Die G├╢tter alle m├╢gen h├╢ren meinen Sang, Sarasvati mit des Gebetes G├╢ttinnen.

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

Wilson

English translation:

тАЬMay the universal gods, accompanied by sacred rites and abundant wisdom, adorable (at thesacrifice) of men, immortal, the knowers of truth, waiting on the oblation to be given, arriving together (at thesacrifice), omniscient, graciously accept all our praises and abundant food with well-sung hymns.тАЭ

Jamison Brereton

All the gods, along with insights and with plenty, worthy of ManuтАЩs sacrifice, immortal, recognizing the truth,
the Escorts and the Gift-Escorts, finding the sun, should take pleasure in the sun, the songs, the sacred formulation, and the hymn.

Griffith

With Holy Thoughts and with Purandhi may all Gods, knowing the Law immortal, Manu’s Holy Ones,
Boon-givers, favourers, finders of light, and Heaven, with gracious love accept my songs, my prayer, my hymn.

Geldner

Alle G├╢tter nebst den frommen Gedanken und der Purandhi, die Opferw├╝rdigen des Manu, die Unsterblichen, Wahrheitskundigen, die mit Gaben Kommenden und ihre Begleiterinnen, die Himmelslichtfinder, die Sonne, sie m├╢gen an den Lobesworten, der erbaulichen Rede, dem Liede Gefallen haben.

Grassmann

Die G├╢tter all’ mit des Gebetes G├╢ttinnen, des Menschen hehre, heilige Unsterblichen, Huldg├╢tter, Gabenspender, Licht verschaffende, der Himmel nehme Lieder, Spruch, Gebete an.

May they this day grant us wide space and freedom: ye Gods, preserve us evermore with blessings.

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рд╡рд╕рд┐рд╖реНрдардГ) рд╕рд░реНрд╡ рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпреЛрдВ рдореЗрдВ рдЕрддреНрдпрдиреНрдд рдмрд╕рд╛ рд╣реБрдЖ (рдЕрдореГрддрд╛рдиреН рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдиреН) рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрдд рд╡рд┐рджреНрд╡рд╛рдиреЛрдВ рдХреЛ (рд╡рд╡рдиреНрджреЗ) рдкреНрд░рд╢рдВрд╕рд┐рдд рдХрд░рддрд╛ рд╣реИ (рдпреЗ рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛ рднреБрд╡рдирд╛-рдЕрднрд┐ рдкреНрд░рддрд╕реНрдереБрдГ) рдЬреЛ рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрдд рд╕рд╛рд░реЗ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдиреЛрдВ рдХреЛ рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░ рдореЗрдВ рд░рдЦрддреЗ рд╣реИрдВ (рддреЗ) рд╡реЗ (рдирдГ) рд╣рдорд╛рд░реЗ рд▓рд┐рдП (рдЕрджреНрдп) рдЖрдЬ-рдЗрд╕ рдЬреАрд╡рди рдореЗрдВ (рдЙрд░реБрдЧрд╛рдпрдВ рд░рд╛рд╕рдиреНрддрд╛рдореН) рдмрд╣реБрдд рдкреНрд░рд╢рдВрд╕рдиреАрдп рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рди-рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдордЬреНрдЮрд╛рди рдХреЛ рджреЗрдВ (рдпреВрдпрдВ рд╕реНрд╡рд╕реНрддрд┐рднрд┐рдГ-рдирдГ рд╕рджрд╛ рдкрд╛рдд) рд╣реЗ рд╡рд┐рджреНрд╡рд╛рдиреЛрдВ ! рддреБрдо рдХрд▓реНрдпрд╛рдгрд╡рдЪрдиреЛрдВ рд╕реЗ рд╣рдореЗрдВ рд╕рджрд╛ рд╕реБрд░рдХреНрд╖рд┐рдд рд░рдЦреЛ реерезрелрее

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рднрд╛рд╡рд╛рд░реНрдерднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - рдирд╡ рд╕реНрдирд╛рддрдХ рд╡рд┐рджреНрд╡рд╛рдиреН рдХреЛ рдЕрдкрдиреА рд╡рд┐рджреНрдпрд╛рд╡реГрджреНрдзрд┐ рдХреЗ рд▓рд┐рдП рдЕрдиреНрдп рдКрдБрдЪреЗ рд╡рд┐рджреНрд╡рд╛рдиреЛрдВ, рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрддреЛрдВ рд╕реЗ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд╡реГрджреНрдзрд┐ рдХрд░рдХреЗ рдЖрддреНрдорд╢рд╛рдиреНрддрд┐ рдкреНрд░рд╛рдкреНрдд рдХрд░рдиреА рдЪрд╛рд╣рд┐рдП, рдЬреЛ рд╕рдмрд╕реЗ рдЙрддреНрдХреГрд╖реНрдЯ рд╡рд╕реНрддреБ рд╣реИ реерезрелрее

рдмреНрд░рд╣реНрдордореБрдирд┐ - рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдердГ

рдкрджрд╛рд░реНрдерд╛рдиреНрд╡рдпрднрд╛рд╖рд╛рдГ - (рд╡рд╕рд┐рд╖реНрдардГ) рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╡рд┐рд╖рдпреЗрд╖реБ рд╡рд╕рд┐рддреГрддрдордГ (рдЕрдореГрддрд╛рдиреН рджреЗрд╡рд╛рдиреН) рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрддрд╛рдиреН рд╡рд┐рджреБрд╖рдГ (рд╡рд╡рдиреНрджреЗ) рдЕрднрд┐рд╡рдиреНрджрддрд┐ (рдпреЗ рд╡рд┐рд╢реНрд╡рд╛ рднреБрд╡рдирд╛-рдЕрднрд┐ рдкреНрд░рддрд╕реНрдереБрдГ) рдпреЗ рдЬреАрд╡рдиреНрдореБрдХреНрддрд╛рдГ рд╕рд░реНрд╡рд╛рдгрд┐ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирд╛рдирд┐-рдЕрдзрд┐рдХрд╛рд░реЗрдг рдкреНрд░рддрд┐рд╖реНрдардиреНрддрд┐ (рддреЗ) рддреЗ рдЦрд▓реБ (рдирдГ) рдЕрд╕реНрдорднреНрдпрдореН (рдЕрджреНрдп) рдЕрд╕реНрдорд┐рдиреН рдХрд╛рд▓реЗ рдЬреАрд╡рдиреЗ (рдЙрд░реБрдЧрд╛рдпрдВ рд░рд╛рд╕рдиреНрддрд╛рдореН) рдмрд╣реБрдкреНрд░рд╢рдВрд╕рдиреАрдпрдВ рдЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдВ рдкрд░рдорд╛рддреНрдордЬреНрдЮрд╛рдирдВ рдкреНрд░рдпрдЪреНрдЫрддреБ (рдпреВрдпрдВ рд╕реНрд╡рд╕реНрддрд┐рднрд┐рдГ-рдирдГ рд╕рджрд╛ рдкрд╛рдд) рд╣реЗ рд╡рд┐рджреНрд╡рд╛рдВрд╕реЛ ! рдпреВрдпрдВ рдХрд▓реНрдпрд╛рдгрд╡рдЪрдиреИрд░рд╕реНрдорд╛рдиреН рд╕рджрд╛ рд░рдХреНрд╖рдд реерезрелрее
